<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item
7.01&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;<u>Regulation FD Disclosure.</u></font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On April 21, 2010, Target Corporation,
through its wholly-owned subsidiaries, Target Receivables Corporation and
Target National Bank, delivered certain monthly reports relating to the
Floating Rate Class A Asset Backed Notes, Series 2005-1, and the Subordinated
Interests, Series 2005-1, issued by the Target Credit Card Owner Trust 2005-1
to the Trustee. These reports are being furnished as exhibits to this report.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As more fully described in the News Releases issued by Target
Corporation on April 6, 2010 and April 14, 2010, Target Corporation&#146;s
wholly-owned subsidiary, Target Receivables Corporation, purchased on April 14,
2010 all of the outstanding Floating Rate Class A Asset backed Notes, Series
2005-1 pursuant to the terms and conditions of a tender offer commenced on April
6, 2010.&#160; Noteholders were paid a
purchase price equal to the principal value along with interest from March 25,
2010 through April 13, 2010.&#160; No further
distributions are due the Noteholders.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item
9.01:&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Financial Statements and
Exhibits</u></font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Arial" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pursuant to the
Amended and Restated Pooling and Servicing Agreement, dated as of
April&nbsp;28, 2000, as amended by Amendment No.&nbsp;1 thereto, dated as of
August&nbsp;22, 2001 (as amended, supplemented or otherwise modified, the &#147;Agreement&#148;),
as supplemented by the Series&nbsp;2005-1 Supplement (as may be amended, from
time to time, the &#147;Series Supplement&#148;), each among Target National Bank, as
Servicer, Target Receivables Corporation, as Transferor, and Wells Fargo Bank,
National Association, as Trustee, the Servicer is required to prepare certain
information each month regarding distributions to Certificateholders and the
performance of the Trust.&#160; The
information with respect to the applicable Distribution Date and Monthly Period
is set forth below.</font></p>
